It continuously watches for changes in the mesh (service registries, Istio configuration resources, endpoint updates) and pushes the translated configuration to all connected proxies via gRPC xDS streams.\n\nThe Discovery Service follows a server-push model: rather than waiting for clients to request updates, Pilot proactively sends configuration changes to all connected proxies. This ensures low-latency propagation of configuration changes across the mesh.\n\n## Architecture Overview Diagram\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                         Istio Configuration                              │\n│    (VirtualService, DestinationRule, ServiceEntry, Gateway, etc.)        │\n│              + Service Registry (K8s Services/Endpoints)                  │\n└──────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                       │ CRD watches + K8s controller watches\n                       ▼\n         ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n         │   Discovery Server (xDS gRPC Server)        │\n         │   - Manages ADS client connections          │\n         │   - Debounces/throttles configuration       │\n         │   - Initializes push context                │\n         └────────────────┬────────────────────────────┘\n                          │\n         ┌────────────────┴────────────────┐\n         │                                 │\n         ▼                                 ▼\n  ┌─────────────────┐          ┌──────────────────────┐\n  │  Push Context   │          │ PushQueue + Push     │\n  │  (Snapshot)     │          │ Coordination         │\n  │                 │          │                      │\n  │ Services        │          │ Rate limiting        │\n  │ VirtualServices │          │ Concurrent push limit│\n  │ DestinationRules│          │ Debouncing           │\n  │ Gateways        │          └──────────┬───────────┘\n  │ Sidecars        │                     │\n  └────────┬────────┘                     │\n           │                              │\n           └──────────────┬───────────────┘\n                          │\n                          ▼\n        ┌──────────────────────────────────────┐\n        │  ADS Connection + Resource Generators│\n        │  (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, SDS, etc.)     │\n        │  Converts PushContext to xDS config  │\n        └──────────────┬───────────────────────┘\n                       │\n        ┌──────────────┴──────────────┐\n        │ Envoy Proxy xDS Connections │\n        ▼                             ▼\n    [Sidecar Pod]              [Sidecar Pod]\n```\n\n---\n\n## 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is Pilot's central gRPC server that implements Envoy's xDS APIs (v3). It is the main coordinator for:\n- Managing active proxy connections\n- Debouncing and throttling configuration updates\n- Creating immutable snapshots (PushContext) when configuration changes\n- Pushing those snapshots to all connected proxies\n\n### Core Responsibilities\n\n#### 1.1 Connection Management\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env *model.Environment\n\n    // Track all active xDS client connections\n    adsClients      map[string]*Connection\n    adsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex\n\n    // Rate limiting for new connection requests\n    RequestRateLimit *rate.Limiter\n\n    // Limit concurrent pushes to avoid overwhelming Pilot\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}\n\n    // ... other fields\n}\n```\n\n**Key Operations:**\n- `addCon()` / `removeCon()` — Register/unregister proxy connections (tracked in `adsClients` map)\n- `Clients()` — Returns all fully initialized connections\n- `AllClients()` — Returns all connections (including uninitialized)\n- `WaitForRequestLimit()` — Enforces rate limiting on new connection requests (prevents thundering herd)\n\n#### 1.2 Configuration Push Coordination\n\nThe Discovery Server coordinates pushes through a multi-stage pipeline:\n\n1. **Event Collection (`pushChannel`):** Configuration updates from watchers (K8s controllers, config CRD watchers) arrive on `pushChannel`\n\n2. **Debouncing (`handleUpdates`):** The `debounce()` function prevents thrashing from rapid successive updates:\n   - `DebounceAfter`: Waits this long before processing (default ~100ms)\n   - `debounceMax`: Maximum wait (default ~10s); forces push if changes keep arriving\n   - Merges multiple update requests received while debouncing into a single push\n   - EDS (endpoint) updates can bypass debouncing with `enableEDSDebounce` flag\n\n3. **Push Context Initialization (`initPushContext`):** Once debounced, a full push generates a new immutable `PushContext`:\n   ```go\n   push := model.NewPushContext()\n   push.InitContext(s.Env, oldPushContext, req)\n   s.Env.SetPushContext(push)\n   ```\n\n4. **Queue and Send (`pushQueue`):** All pending connections are enqueued in `PushQueue`, which:\n   - Respects `concurrentPushLimit` (semaphore) to avoid overwhelming Pilot\n   - Calls `pushConnection()` for each proxy to generate and send xDS resources\n\n#### 1.3 xDS Protocol Implementation\n\nThe Discovery Server implements three xDS modes:\n\n- **Aggregated Discovery Service (ADS):** Bidirectional gRPC stream where both client and server can send messages\n  - Implemented in `ads.go` as `StreamAggregatedResources()`\n  - Single stream carries all resource types (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, SDS, etc.)\n  - Envoy can request specific resources or resource updates\n\n- **State-of-the-World (SotW):** Full resource set sent on each update (default)\n  - All matching resources for a type sent in one response\n  - Higher overhead but simpler\n\n- **Incremental/Delta:** Only changed resources sent\n  - Implemented in `delta.go` as `DeltaAggregatedResources()`\n  - Newer, more efficient protocol\n  - Uses the `Delta` field in `PushRequest` to track subscriptions\n\n#### 1.4 Cache Management\n\n```go\nCache model.XdsCache\n```\n\nThe DiscoveryServer maintains a cache of generated xDS resources:\n- **Purpose:** Avoid recomputing the same xDS resources for multiple proxies\n- **Invalidation:** On config changes, `dropCacheForRequest()` clears cache entries\n- **Lazy computation:** Generators compute resources on-demand and cache the results\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`\n\nThe ADS module handles the bidirectional gRPC stream between Pilot and each Envoy proxy, including request processing and push delivery.\n\n### 2.1 Stream Establishment (`Stream()` / `StreamAggregatedResources()`)\n\nWhen an Envoy proxy connects:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n    // 1. Rate limit check\n    if err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(stream.Context()); err != nil {\n        return status.Errorf(codes.ResourceExhausted, \"...\")\n    }\n\n    // 2. Authentication (mTLS identity verification)\n    ids, err := s.authenticate(ctx)\n\n    // 3. Ensure push context is ready\n    s.globalPushContext().InitContext(s.Env, nil, nil)\n\n    // 4. Create connection wrapper\n    con := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n    con.ids = ids\n    con.s = s\n\n    // 5. Delegate to xds.Stream for handling the connection lifecycle\n    return xds.Stream(con)\n}\n```\n\nThe connection lifecycle:\n1. **Initialize:** `initConnection()` extracts proxy metadata from the first request\n2. **Track:** `addCon()` registers the connection in `adsClients`\n3. **Serve:** `xds.Stream()` handles bidirectional message exchange\n4. **Close:** `removeCon()` cleans up when stream ends\n\n### 2.2 Connection Type and Proxy State\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection              // Base gRPC stream wrapper\n\n    node *core.Node             // Original Envoy node metadata\n    proxy *model.Proxy          // Parsed proxy identity and configuration\n\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream  // For delta xDS (if used)\n    deltaReqChan chan *discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest\n\n    s *DiscoveryServer\n    ids []string                // Authenticated identities (from mTLS)\n}\n```\n\n**Proxy State:** Each connection manages a `model.Proxy` object containing:\n- Proxy metadata: ID, cluster, namespace, IP addresses\n- Service targets: Which services this proxy can access\n- Workload labels: Pod labels, locality information\n- Watched resources: Which xDS resource types this proxy is subscribed to\n- Cached push context: Last configuration version sent to this proxy\n\n### 2.3 Request Processing (`processRequest()`)\n\nWhen Envoy sends an xDS request:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n    stype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)\n    log.Debugf(\"ADS:%s: REQ %s resources:%d\", stype, con.ID(), len(req.ResourceNames))\n\n    // Update proxy's watched resource for this type\n    shouldRespond, delta := xds.ShouldRespond(con.proxy, con.ID(), req)\n    if !shouldRespond {\n        return nil  // ACK'd by proxy, no new data needed\n    }\n\n    // Create a push request from this client request\n    request := &model.PushRequest{\n        Full:   true,\n        Push:   con.proxy.LastPushContext,\n        Reason: model.NewReasonStats(model.ProxyRequest),\n        Delta:  delta,  // Resource subscription delta\n        Forced: true,\n    }\n\n    // Generate and send the requested resource type\n    return s.pushXds(con, con.proxy.GetWatchedResource(req.TypeUrl), request)\n}\n```\n\n**Request Handling:**\n- Envoy sends `DiscoveryRequest` with: `TypeUrl` (resource type), `ResourceNames` (which resources), `VersionInfo` (last version ACK'd), `ResponseNonce` (request number)\n- Pilot checks if Envoy already has latest version; if so, ACKs and moves on\n- Otherwise, generates the requested resources and sends `DiscoveryResponse`\n\n### 2.4 Push Delivery (`pushConnection()`)\n\nWhen a configuration change triggers a fleet-wide push:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) pushConnection(con *Connection, pushEv *Event) error {\n    pushRequest := pushEv.pushRequest\n\n    if pushRequest.Full {\n        // Update proxy state (service targets, sidecar scope, etc.)\n        s.computeProxyState(con.proxy, pushRequest)\n    }\n\n    // Check if this proxy actually needs updates\n    pushRequest, needsPush := s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushRequest)\n    if !needsPush {\n        return nil  // Skip push for this proxy\n    }\n\n    // Send all watched resource types in order: CDS → EDS → LDS → RDS → SDS → ...\n    wrl := con.watchedResourcesByOrder()\n    for _, w := range wrl {\n        if err := s.pushXds(con, w, pushRequest); err != nil {\n            return err\n        }\n    }\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n**Push Ordering:** `PushOrder` defines the order xDS resources are sent:\n1. **CDS** (Clusters): Service discovery, load balancing endpoints\n2. **EDS** (Endpoints): Which instances (IPs/ports) are available\n3. **LDS** (Listeners): Which ports to listen on, filter chains\n4. **RDS** (Routes): HTTP routing rules\n5. **SDS** (Secrets): TLS certificates\n6. **Address, Workload, WorkloadAuthorization** (for ambient mesh)\n\nThis order is critical: Envoy requires CDS before EDS, and LDS before RDS.\n\n### 2.5 StartPush — Broadcast to All Proxies\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) StartPush(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    req.Start = time.Now()\n    for _, p := range s.AllClients() {\n        s.pushQueue.Enqueue(p, req)\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWhen a configuration change occurs, `StartPush()` enqueues the same `PushRequest` for every connected proxy. The `PushQueue` then distributes pushes, respecting concurrency limits.\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\nThe `PushContext` is an immutable snapshot of the entire mesh configuration at a specific point in time. It is created when configuration changes and used during the push phase to generate xDS resources for all proxies.\n\n### 3.1 PushContext Data Structure\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service index\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex\n\n    // Configuration indexes\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex\n\n    // Policy indexes\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies\n    Telemetry *Telemetries\n    ProxyConfigs *ProxyConfigs\n\n    // Mesh configuration\n    Mesh *meshconfig.MeshConfig\n    Networks *meshconfig.MeshNetworks\n\n    // Push metadata\n    PushVersion string  // Unique identifier for this push context\n\n    // Status tracking\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n}\n```\n\n**Purpose:** Rather than each resource generator re-querying the config store, they access pre-indexed data from `PushContext`. This:\n- Improves performance (avoid repeated lookups)\n- Ensures consistency (all generators see the same config snapshot)\n- Enables efficient scoping (e.g., which VirtualServices apply to which proxies)\n\n### 3.2 Context Initialization (`InitContext()`)\n\nWhen a configuration change occurs, a new `PushContext` is created and initialized:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) {\n    ps.Mesh = env.Mesh()\n    ps.Networks = env.MeshNetworks()\n\n    ps.initDefaultExportMaps()\n\n    // Full rebuild or incremental update?\n    if pushReq == nil || oldPushContext == nil || !oldPushContext.InitDone.Load() || pushReq.Forced {\n        ps.createNewContext(env)  // Full rebuild\n    } else {\n        ps.updateContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq)  // Incremental\n    }\n\n    ps.InitDone.Store(true)\n}\n```\n\n**Full Rebuild (`createNewContext`):**\nRebuilds all indexes from scratch. Called when:\n- Initial push context creation\n- Full push triggered (e.g., due to mesh configuration change)\n- Forced push\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) createNewContext(env *Environment) {\n    ps.initServiceRegistry(env, nil)      // Load services from K8s + ServiceEntry\n    ps.initVirtualServices(env)           // Index VirtualServices\n    ps.initDestinationRules(env)          // Index DestinationRules\n    ps.initAuthnPolicies(env)             // Authentication policies\n    ps.initAuthorizationPolicies(env)     // Authorization policies\n    ps.initTelemetry(env)                 // Telemetry configuration\n    ps.initWasmPlugins(env)               // WASM plugin configuration\n    ps.initEnvoyFilters(env, nil, nil)   // Envoy filters\n    ps.initGateways(env)                  // Gateway configurations\n    ps.initSidecarScopes(env)             // Sidecar scopes (MUST be last)\n}\n```\n\n**Incremental Update (`updateContext`):**\nOnly rebuilds indexes for changed resource types. Example:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) updateContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) {\n    // Check which types changed\n    for conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n        switch conf.Kind {\n        case kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DNSName:\n            servicesChanged = true\n        case kind.VirtualService:\n            virtualServicesChanged = true\n        case kind.DestinationRule:\n            destinationRulesChanged = true\n        // ... etc\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Only rebuild affected indexes\n    if servicesChanged {\n        ps.initServiceRegistry(env, pushReq.ConfigsUpdated)\n    } else {\n        ps.ServiceIndex = oldPushContext.ServiceIndex  // Reuse\n    }\n\n    if virtualServicesChanged {\n        ps.initVirtualServices(env)\n    } else {\n        ps.virtualServiceIndex = oldPushContext.virtualServiceIndex  // Reuse\n    }\n    // ... similar for other types\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Configuration Translation: From Istio Config to xDS\n\nThe `PushContext` contains pre-indexed Istio configuration. **Generators** use this during xDS generation to translate Istio config → Envoy config:\n\n**Example: RouteConfiguration (RDS) Generation**\n- Input: `PushContext.virtualServiceIndex` (VirtualServices) + `PushContext.destinationRuleIndex` (DestinationRules)\n- Process: For each proxy, select applicable VirtualServices (matching hostname, gateway) and merge DestinationRules\n- Output: Envoy `RouteConfiguration` with routes, weighted clusters, traffic policies\n\n**Example: Cluster (CDS) Generation**\n- Input: `PushContext.ServiceIndex` (Services from K8s + ServiceEntry)\n- Process: For each service, create Envoy Cluster with load balancing settings from DestinationRules\n- Output: Envoy `Cluster` with endpoint discovery (EDS), outlier detection, connection pooling\n\n**Example: Endpoint (EDS) Generation**\n- Input: `PushContext.ServiceIndex` + current endpoints from service registry\n- Process: Fetch endpoints for requested cluster, apply subset selection from DestinationRules\n- Output: Envoy `ClusterLoadAssignment` with endpoint list and health information\n\n### 3.4 Service Registry Index (`ServiceIndex`)\n\n```go\ntype serviceIndex struct {\n    // Services scoped to single namespace (exportTo \".\")\n    privateByNamespace map[string][]*Service\n\n    // Services visible mesh-wide (exportTo \"*\")\n    public []*Service\n\n    // Services exported to specific namespaces\n    exportedToNamespace map[string][]*Service\n\n    // Lookup table: hostname + namespace → service\n    HostnameAndNamespace map[host.Name]map[string]*Service\n\n    // Cache of endpoints per port\n    instancesByPort map[string]map[int][]*IstioEndpoint\n}\n```\n\nThe service index is populated by `initServiceRegistry()`:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) initServiceRegistry(env *Environment, configsUpdate sets.Set[ConfigKey]) {\n    allServices := SortServicesByCreationTime(env.Services())\n\n    for _, s := range allServices {\n        // Determine which namespaces can access this service (based on exportTo)\n        visibleNamespaces := getVisibleNamespaces(s)\n\n        // Index the service\n        for _, ns := range visibleNamespaces {\n            ps.ServiceIndex.addService(ns, s)\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis index is queried during request processing:\n- CDS generator calls `GetServices()` to list all services for a cluster\n- RDS generator calls `GetAggregatedServices()` to find services matching a hostname\n- EDS generator calls `GetAggregatedInstances()` to fetch endpoints for a service\n\n### 3.5 Metrics and Error Tracking\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n}\n\ntype ProxyPushStatus struct {\n    ClusterSent       int\n    ClusterAckeded    int\n    ClusterNacked     int\n    EndpointSent      int\n    // ... per-resource-type counts\n}\n```\n\nAfter each push, Pilot updates `ProxyStatus` to track:\n- How many resources sent to each proxy\n- How many ACKs/NACKs received\n- Any errors during generation\n\nThese metrics are exposed via debug endpoints and used for operational visibility.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`\n\nThe Service Registry layer provides service discovery to the xDS generators. It watches Kubernetes Services, Endpoints, and ServiceEntry resources, and triggers configuration updates when they change.\n\n### 4.1 Multi-Registry Pattern\n\nIstio supports multiple concurrent service registries:\n\n```\n┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│           Aggregate Controller                                  │\n│  (pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go)           │\n│                                                                 │\n│  Queries and aggregates from multiple providers:               │\n│  ├── Kubernetes Service Registry (current cluster)             │\n│  ├── Kubernetes Service Registry (remote cluster 1)            │\n│  ├── Kubernetes Service Registry (remote cluster 2)            │\n│  ├── ServiceEntry Registry                                     │\n│  └── External service providers (extensible)                   │\n└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n         │                    │                    │\n         ▼                    ▼                    ▼\n┌─────────────────┐  ┌──────────────────┐  ┌──────────────────┐\n│ Kube Controller │  │  Kube Controller │  │ ServiceEntry     │\n│ (Local Cluster) │  │  (Remote Cluster)│  │ Controller       │\n│                 │  │                  │  │                  │\n│ Watches:        │  │ Watches:         │  │ Watches:         │\n│ - Services      │  │ - Services       │  │ - ServiceEntry   │\n│ - Endpoints     │  │ - Endpoints      │  │ - WorkloadEntry  │\n│ - Pods          │  │ - Pods           │  │ (via API server) │\n└─────────────────┘  └──────────────────┘  └──────────────────┘\n```\n\n**Aggregate Controller** (`pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go`):\n- Maintains a list of active registries\n- Implements `ServiceDiscovery` interface by delegating to each registry\n- Merges results (e.g., when finding a service, check all registries)\n- Broadcasts events from any registry to the XDS updater\n\n### 4.2 Kubernetes Service Registry\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go`\n\nWatches Kubernetes resources and converts them to Istio's internal service model:\n\n**Watches:**\n- **Service** → `model.Service` (service definition)\n- **EndpointSlice/Endpoints** → `model.IstioEndpoint` (pods/endpoints)\n- **Pod** → Adds labels, locality information\n\n**Conversion:**\n```go\nService (K8s) → model.Service\n    - Kubernetes ClusterIP → Istio Service hostname\n    - Service ports → Istio Service ports\n    - Labels → Service attributes\n\nPod → model.IstioEndpoint\n    - Pod IP → endpoint address\n    - Container ports → endpoint ports\n    - Pod labels → endpoint labels (used for subset selection)\n    - Pod node → locality (region/zone/subzone)\n```\n\n**Updates Triggered:**\n- `ServiceAdded(shard, service)` — New service discovered\n- `ServiceDeleted(shard, service)` — Service removed\n- `ServiceUpdated(shard, service)` — Service modified (e.g., port added)\n- `WorkloadHealthCheckChanged()` — Pod health status changed (for outlier detection)\n\n### 4.3 ServiceEntry Registry\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/serviceentry/`\n\nHandles Istio's `ServiceEntry` and `WorkloadEntry` custom resources:\n\n**ServiceEntry:** Manually register external services (outside K8s)\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: ServiceEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: external-api\nspec:\n  hosts:\n  - api.example.com\n  location: MESH_EXTERNAL  # Or MESH_INTERNAL\n  ports:\n  - name: https\n    number: 443\n    protocol: HTTPS\n  endpoints:\n  - address: 192.0.2.1\n    labels:\n      version: v1\n```\n\n**WorkloadEntry:** Register individual workloads for auto-registration\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: WorkloadEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: vm-service\nspec:\n  address: 192.0.2.10\n  labels:\n    app: my-service\n```\n\nThe ServiceEntry controller converts these to service/endpoint objects that other components can consume.\n\n### 4.4 Multi-Cluster Support\n\nPilot can connect to multiple Kubernetes clusters and aggregate their services:\n\n**Configuration:**\n```go\n// Pilot running on cluster \"primary\"\nregistries := []*registryEntry{\n    &registryEntry{\n        registry: primaryKubeRegistry,\n        clusterID: \"primary\",\n    },\n    &registryEntry{\n        registry: remoteKubeRegistry,\n        clusterID: \"remote-east\",\n    },\n}\naggregateController := aggregate.NewController(registries)\n```\n\n**Service Aggregation:**\nWhen looking up a hostname, the aggregate controller queries all registries:\n\n```\nClient requests \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n└─→ Query K8s primary cluster\n    └─→ Found: [10.0.1.2, 10.0.1.3] (reviews pods in primary)\n└─→ Query K8s remote cluster\n    └─→ Found: [10.1.2.4, 10.1.2.5] (reviews pods in remote)\n└─→ Result: All 4 endpoints available for load balancing\n```\n\n**Network Awareness:**\nEach endpoint is tagged with its network and cluster:\n- Endpoints in the same network as the client are preferred (lower latency)\n- Istio uses locality-based load balancing to favor local endpoints\n- Cross-network traffic routes through gateways (if configured)\n\n### 4.5 Endpoint Discovery and EDS Updates\n\nEndpoints are tracked by **shard** (registry + cluster):\n\n```go\ntype ShardKey struct {\n    Cluster cluster.ID  // \"primary\", \"remote-east\", etc.\n    // implicitly: registry provider (Kubernetes, ServiceEntry, etc.)\n}\n```\n\nWhen endpoints change:\n\n```\nPod scales up: 10.0.1.2 added to reviews\n└─→ K8s watcher fires EndpointSlice change event\n└─→ Kube controller calls xdsUpdater.EDSUpdate()\n    └─→ Populates: shard=K8s/primary, hostname=reviews,\n                   endpoints=[10.0.1.2, 10.0.1.3, 10.0.1.4]\n    └─→ Triggers: pushRequest with reason=EDS\n        └─→ Only EDS is pushed (not full push)\n        └─→ Only proxies targeting this service get updated\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Data Flow: Configuration Change to xDS Push\n\n### 5.1 Full Push Flow: Config Change → Envoy\n\n```\n1. CONFIG CHANGE\n   ├─ User creates/updates VirtualService\n   ├─ Or K8s applies ServiceEntry\n   └─ Pilot's config store watcher detects change\n\n2. WATCH EVENT\n   └─ `ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest)` called\n      ├─ ConfigsUpdated = {VirtualService/my-vs}\n      └─ Full = true (rebuild context)\n\n3. DEBOUNCE (in handleUpdates goroutine)\n   ├─ Event added to pushChannel\n   ├─ Waits DebounceAfter (e.g., 100ms)\n   ├─ If no new events, proceeds to next step\n   ├─ If new events, resets timer (up to debounceMax of ~10s)\n   └─ Multiple events merged into single PushRequest\n\n4. PUSH CONTEXT INIT\n   └─ `initPushContext(req)` called\n      ├─ Creates new PushContext\n      ├─ Calls `InitContext(env, oldContext, req)`\n         ├─ Determines if full or incremental rebuild\n         ├─ If incremental: checks ConfigsUpdated kinds\n         │  ├─ VirtualService changed? rebuild virtualServiceIndex\n         │  ├─ ServiceEntry changed? rebuild ServiceIndex\n         │  └─ Reuse other indexes from oldContext\n         ├─ If full: rebuilds all indexes\n         └─ Sets InitDone=true\n      ├─ Updates global PushContext (stored in Environment)\n      └─ Clears cache entries related to changed configs\n\n5. FLUSH QUEUE (sendPushes goroutine)\n   └─ For each connected proxy (from Clients() list):\n      ├─ Enqueue(proxy, pushRequest) into PushQueue\n      └─ Semaphore respects concurrent push limit\n\n6. GENERATE XDS (doSendPushes goroutine for each proxy)\n   ├─ Read from PushQueue\n   ├─ Call `pushConnection(con, event)`\n   │  ├─ Update proxy state: computeProxyState()\n   │  │  ├─ Set service targets (which services affect this proxy)\n   │  │  ├─ Compute sidecar scope\n   │  │  └─ Set workload labels/locality\n   │  ├─ Check ProxyNeedsPush() — skip if no relevant changes\n   │  └─ For each watched resource type (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, SDS):\n   │     └─ Call `pushXds(con, watchedResource, pushRequest)`\n   │        ├─ Find generator for resource type\n   │        ├─ Generator.Generate(proxy, watchedResource, pushRequest)\n   │        │  └─ Uses PushContext to build xDS resource\n   │        │     ├─ CDS: Queries ServiceIndex, applies DestinationRules\n   │        │     ├─ LDS: Queries SidecarScope, Gateways\n   │        │     ├─ RDS: Queries VirtualServices + DestinationRules\n   │        │     └─ EDS: Queries ServiceIndex for endpoints\n   │        ├─ Construct DiscoveryResponse\n   │        ├─ Send via gRPC stream: xds.Send(con, resp)\n   │        └─ Log: \"CDS: PUSH for proxy-id resources:5 size:2.3KB\"\n   └─ Mark push done, release semaphore\n\n7. ENVOY RECEIVES & ACKs\n   ├─ Envoy receives DiscoveryResponse(TypeUrl=CDS, VersionInfo=v42)\n   ├─ Validates clusters\n   ├─ Sends back DiscoveryRequest(TypeUrl=CDS, VersionInfo=v42, ResponseNonce=nonce42)\n   └─ Pilot logs: \"CDS: ACK from proxy-id\"\n```\n\n### 5.2 Incremental Push Flow: Endpoint Change\n\n```\n1. ENDPOINT CHANGE\n   └─ Pod scales from 2 → 3 replicas\n      ├─ K8s updates Endpoint/EndpointSlice\n      └─ Kube controller detects change\n\n2. EDS UPDATE\n   └─ `EDSUpdate(shard=K8s/cluster-1, hostname=reviews, endpoints=[...])`\n      ├─ Updates endpoint cache\n      ├─ Calls `ConfigUpdate(&model.PushRequest{Full: false})`\n      └─ Reason = EDS\n\n3. DEBOUNCE (if EDS debounce enabled)\n   └─ Similar to config change, but Full=false\n\n4. NO CONTEXT REBUILD\n   └─ Full=false, so skip `initPushContext()`\n      ├─ Reuse global PushContext\n      └─ Only clear EDS cache\n\n5. INCREMENTAL PUSH\n   └─ `AdsPushAll(req)` with Full=false\n      └─ For each proxy:\n         ├─ Enqueue(proxy, req)\n         └─ In `pushConnection()`:\n            ├─ Skip `computeProxyState()` (Full=false)\n            ├─ Only push EDS (skipped by generators: cdsNeedsPush, rdsNeedsPush, etc.)\n            └─ `pushXds(con, EDS)`\n               └─ Send only EDS response with new endpoints\n\n6. ENVOY UPDATES LOAD BALANCER\n   └─ Receives EDS update\n      ├─ Adds new endpoint\n      └─ Immediately available for traffic\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Extension Points\n\nIstio provides several extension points for customization:\n\n### 6.1 Custom Resource Generators\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:Generators`\n\n```go\nGenerators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator\n```\n\nUsers can replace or supplement the default xDS generators:\n\n```go\ntype XdsResourceGenerator interface {\n    Generate(proxy *Proxy, watched *WatchedResource, req *PushRequest) (model.Resources, model.LogData, error)\n}\n```\n\n**Example Use Cases:**\n- Add custom routing logic beyond VirtualService\n- Integrate external service mesh or configuration system\n- Generate Envoy filters dynamically\n- Apply organization-specific policies\n\n**Usage:**\n```go\nds.Generators[\"custom\"] = &MyCustomGenerator{...}\n\n// Envoy specifies generator via metadata:\n// node.metadata.GENERATOR = \"custom\"\n```\n\n### 6.2 Config Translation Layer\n\nResource generators translate Istio config → Envoy config. The default generators are in:\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/*.go` — Core networking logic\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/*.go` — xDS generation (cds.go, rds.go, lds.go, eds.go, sds.go)\n\n**Hook Points:**\n- **Pre-generation:** Filter which services/routes apply to a proxy (via SidecarScope)\n- **Generation:** Apply TrafficPolicy, PeerAuthentication, AuthorizationPolicy\n- **Post-generation:** EnvoyFilter can add/modify Envoy resources\n\n### 6.3 Service Discovery Integration\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`\n\nTo integrate a custom service registry (e.g., Consul, external API):\n\n```go\ntype ServiceDiscovery interface {\n    Services() []*Service\n    GetService(hostname host.Name) *Service\n    InstancesByPort(hostname host.Name, port int, labels labels.Collection) []*IstioEndpoint\n    // ... etc\n}\n```\n\nRegister with aggregate controller:\n```go\ncustomRegistry := &MyCustomRegistry{...}\naggregateController.AddRegistry(customRegistry)\n```\n\nOn service/endpoint changes, call:\n```go\nxdsUpdater.SvcUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, event)\nxdsUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n```\n\n### 6.4 Proxy Customization Filter\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:ProxyNeedsPush`\n\nUsers can filter whether a proxy needs updates:\n\n```go\nProxyNeedsPush func(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) (*model.PushRequest, bool)\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```go\nds.ProxyNeedsPush = func(proxy *Proxy, req *PushRequest) (*PushRequest, bool) {\n    // Skip push to this proxy if it's not in the right zone\n    if !isInZone(proxy, targetZone) {\n        return req, false  // Skip\n    }\n    return req, true  // Process\n}\n```\n\n### 6.5 Authentication & Authorization\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/auth.go`\n\nThe DiscoveryServer supports multiple authenticators for mTLS verification:\n\n```go\nAuthenticators []security.Authenticator\n```\n\nCustom authenticators can be added:\n```go\nds.Authenticators = append(ds.Authenticators, &MyCustomAuthenticator{...})\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Error Handling\n\n### 7.1 Config Validation Errors\n\nWhen Istio configuration is invalid (e.g., malformed YAML, invalid field values):\n\n**Detection:** Config store watchers validate on create/update\n**Impact:** Invalid resource is rejected by Kubernetes API server\n**Pilot Behavior:** Skips the invalid resource; continues with others\n\n### 7.2 Push Generation Errors\n\nWhen a generator fails to produce xDS resources for a proxy:\n\n```go\nres, logdata, err := gen.Generate(con.proxy, w, req)\nif err != nil || res == nil {\n    log.Debugf(\"%s: SKIP for node:%s\", typeUrl, con.ID())\n    return err  // Error logged, no response sent\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:** Proxy doesn't receive update for that resource type; retains previous version\n\n### 7.3 Network Transmission Errors\n\nIf `xds.Send(con, resp)` fails (network down, stream closed):\n\n```go\nif err := xds.Send(con, resp); err != nil {\n    log.Warnf(\"%s: Send failure for node:%s: %v\", typeUrl, con.ID(), err)\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n**Impact:**\n- Push aborted for remaining resources\n- Connection loop terminates\n- Proxy reconnects (exponential backoff)\n\n### 7.4 Proxy Disconnection\n\nWhen a proxy stream closes:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) closeConnection(con *Connection) {\n    if con.ID() == \"\" {\n        return\n    }\n    s.removeCon(con.ID())  // Untrack from adsClients\n    s.WorkloadEntryController.OnDisconnect(con)\n}\n```\n\n**Cleanup:**\n- Connection removed from `adsClients` map\n- No further pushes enqueued for this proxy\n- Auto-registration (WorkloadEntry) cleaned up\n\n### 7.5 Rate Limiting & Overload Protection\n\n```go\n// Limit concurrent pushes\nconcurrentPushLimit chan struct{}\n\n// Limit new connection requests\nRequestRateLimit *rate.Limiter\n```\n\nIf Pilot receives too many new connections:\n```go\nif err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(stream.Context()); err != nil {\n    return status.Errorf(codes.ResourceExhausted, \"request rate limit exceeded\")\n}\n```\n\nIf too many concurrent pushes:\n```go\nsemaphore <- struct{}{}  // Blocks if concurrentPushLimit is full\n// ... perform push ...\n<-semaphore  // Release\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Key Data Structures and Interfaces\n\n### 8.1 Model.PushRequest\n\nRepresents a request to push configuration:\n\n```go\ntype PushRequest struct {\n    Full bool  // Full or incremental push?\n\n    ConfigsUpdated sets.Set[ConfigKey]  // Which configs changed (VirtualService, ServiceEntry, etc.)\n    AddressesUpdated sets.Set[string]   // Which addresses (IPs) changed\n\n    Push *PushContext  // Configuration snapshot to use for generation\n\n    Start time.Time    // When this push was queued\n    Reason ReasonStats // Why: ProxyRequest, ConfigChange, ServiceUpdate, etc.\n\n    Delta ResourceDelta  // For incremental xDS: subscribed/unsubscribed resources\n\n    Forced bool  // Ignore caches, force generation\n}\n```\n\n### 8.2 Model.Proxy\n\nRepresents a connected proxy:\n\n```go\ntype Proxy struct {\n    ID string  // \"cluster-1/namespace/pod-name\"\n\n    Type ProxyType  // Sidecar, Router, Ztunnel, Waypoint\n\n    Metadata ProxyMetadata  // From Envoy node metadata\n        ClusterID cluster.ID\n        Namespace string\n        // ... etc\n\n    IPAddresses []string\n    Locality *Locality  // Region/Zone/SubZone\n\n    ServiceTargets []*Service  // Which services affect this proxy\n    SidecarScope *SidecarScope  // Which config applies to this proxy\n\n    WatchedResources map[string]*WatchedResource  // Subscribed to which xDS types\n\n    LastPushContext *PushContext  // Last config used for this proxy\n    LastPushTime time.Time\n}\n```\n\n### 8.3 Model.Service\n\nRepresents a service in the mesh:\n\n```go\ntype Service struct {\n    Hostname host.Name  // \"reviews.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n    Namespace string\n\n    Ports []*Port\n        Name string\n        Port int\n        Protocol string\n\n    Attributes ServiceAttributes\n        ExportTo sets.Set[Namespace]  // Which namespaces can access\n        // ... etc\n\n    ClusterVIPs map[cluster.ID]string  // Cluster IP in each cluster\n}\n```\n\n### 8.4 Model.IstioEndpoint\n\nRepresents an individual endpoint (pod/VM):\n\n```go\ntype IstioEndpoint struct {\n    Address string  // \"10.0.1.2\"\n    Port int        // 8080\n\n    Labels labels.Instance  // Pod labels (for subset selection)\n\n    Locality *Locality  // Region/Zone\n\n    ClusterID cluster.ID  // \"primary\", \"remote-east\"\n    Network string        // \"network-1\"\n\n    TLSMode string  // \"ISTIO\", \"DISABLED\", \"PERMISSIVE\"\n\n    WorkloadName string  // For ambient workloads\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Performance Considerations\n\n### 9.1 Debouncing\n\nPrevents thrashing from rapid updates:\n- Default: Wait 100ms after first change\n- Maximum: Wait 10s (force push if changes keep arriving)\n- Benefit: Reduces CPU, network traffic\n- Cost: ~100ms additional latency on config changes\n\n### 9.2 Incremental vs. Full Pushes\n\n**Incremental Pushes (EDS):**\n- Only changed endpoints sent\n- PushContext **not** rebuilt\n- Much faster (~10ms vs 500ms for full push)\n- Used for endpoint changes (pods scaling, health changes)\n\n**Full Pushes:**\n- All xDS resources regenerated\n- PushContext rebuilt (indexes all config)\n- Slower but necessary when structural config changes\n\n### 9.3 Caching\n\n- XDS resources cached after generation\n- Cache keys: (ProxyID, ResourceType, ResourceNames)\n- Cleared on config changes to affected types\n- Benefit: Proxies with identical config get cached results\n\n### 9.4 Concurrent Push Limiting\n\nPilot spawns a goroutine for each proxy push. To avoid overwhelming Pilot:\n\n```go\n// Default: 5 concurrent pushes\nconcurrentPushLimit: make(chan struct{}, features.PushThrottle)\n```\n\nExcess pushes wait in queue until earlier pushes complete.\n\n### 9.5 Proxy Filtering\n\nNot all proxies need all config changes:\n\n```go\n// Example: ServiceEntry change only affects proxies that can reach that service\nif req.ConfigsUpdated.Contains(ServiceEntry/my-external-api) {\n    // Only notify proxies in namespaces that can access the API namespace\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Relevant Source Files\n\n### Core xDS Server\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` — DiscoveryServer, push coordination\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` — ADS stream handling, connection lifecycle\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/xdsgen.go` — XDS generation pipeline\n\n### Resource Generators\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` — Cluster Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` — Listener Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` — Route Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` — Endpoint Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/sds.go` — Secret Discovery Service generator\n\n### Configuration Model\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` — PushContext and config indexing\n- `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` — Service and endpoint model\n- `pilot/pkg/model/proxy_config.go` — Proxy state management\n\n### Service Registry\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` — Multi-registry aggregation\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go` — Kubernetes service discovery\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/serviceentry/controller.go` — ServiceEntry/WorkloadEntry support\n\n### Utilities\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go` — Push queue management\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eventhandler.go` — Configuration event handling\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/` — Config generation utilities\n\n---\n\n## 11. Extension Examples\n\n### Example 1: Custom Service Registry\n\n```go\ntype ConsulRegistry struct {\n    consulClient *api.Client\n}\n\nfunc (c *ConsulRegistry) Services() []*model.Service {\n    // Query Consul for services\n    services, _ := c.consulClient.Catalog().Services(nil)\n    return convertToIstioServices(services)\n}\n\nfunc (c *ConsulRegistry) GetService(hostname host.Name) *model.Service {\n    // Lookup single service\n}\n\n// Register with Pilot\naggregateController.AddRegistry(&ConsulRegistry{...})\n```\n\n### Example 2: Custom Config Generator\n\n```go\ntype CustomRDSGenerator struct{}\n\nfunc (g *CustomRDSGenerator) Generate(proxy *model.Proxy, w *model.WatchedResource, req *model.PushRequest) (model.Resources, model.LogData, error) {\n    // Access PushContext for VirtualServices, DestinationRules\n    push := req.Push\n\n    // Custom routing logic\n    routes := []proto.Message{}\n    for _, vs := range push.GetVirtualServices() {\n        if appliesToProxy(vs, proxy) {\n            route := buildCustomRoute(vs, push)\n            routes = append(routes, route)\n        }\n    }\n\n    return convertToResources(routes), model.LogData{}, nil\n}\n```\n\n### Example 3: Monitoring Push Events\n\n```go\noriginalPushConnection := ds.pushConnection\nds.pushConnection = func(con *Connection, pushEv *Event) error {\n    start := time.Now()\n    err := originalPushConnection(con, pushEv)\n    duration := time.Since(start)\n\n    // Record metric\n    pushDurationMetric.WithLabelValues(con.proxy.ID).Observe(duration.Seconds())\n\n    return err\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nIstio Pilot's Discovery Service is a sophisticated, high-performance system for configuration distribution:\n\n1. **DiscoveryServer** coordinates the push lifecycle: receives config changes, debounces them, creates immutable snapshots (PushContext), and distributes them to proxies\n\n2. **ADS** implements the bidirectional gRPC protocol for streaming xDS configuration to Envoy proxies, handling request processing and push delivery\n\n3. **PushContext** is an immutable configuration snapshot containing indexed services, routes, policies, etc. that generators use to create xDS resources\n\n4. **Service Registry** watches Kubernetes resources and custom ServiceEntries, providing service discovery across multiple clusters and registries\n\n5. **Generators** translate Istio's high-level config (VirtualService, DestinationRule, etc.) into low-level Envoy configuration (RDS routes, CDS clusters, EDS endpoints)\n\nThe system is optimized for scale:\n- Debouncing reduces thrashing\n- Incremental pushes avoid full context rebuilds\n- Caching avoids redundant generation\n- Concurrent limits prevent overload\n- Proxy filtering avoids unnecessary updates\n\nThe architecture is also designed for extensibility:\n- Custom service registries can be plugged in\n- Resource generators can be overridden\n- Proxy filtering can be customized\n- Authentication can be extended\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

It continuously watches for changes in the mesh (service registries, Istio configuration resources, endpoint updates) and pushes the translated configuration to all connected proxies via gRPC xDS streams.\n\nThe Discovery Service follows a server-push model: rather than waiting for clients to request updates, Pilot proactively sends configuration changes to all connected proxies.
